# Telegram Stock-Mention Watch

> State file for [Routine 6 — Telegram Stock-Mention Scan](../../framework/automation-schedule.md#routine-6--telegram-stock-mention-scan) (`/telegram-scan`). Overwritten in place each run — git history preserves prior state, same convention as [ibkr.md](ibkr.md) and [ibkr-orders.md](ibkr-orders.md). Tracks the last-seen post per monitored channel (so no post is reprocessed or silently skipped) plus a running log of every company mention the command has evaluated, whether or not it triggered an action.

TLS connect error: ... OPENSSL_internal: invalid library`. Diagnosed as an environment-level incompatibility, not a transient fault: yfinance's underlying `curl_cffi` library performs browser-TLS-fingerprint impersonation via its own bundled TLS stack, which this session's policy-enforcing proxy (see `/root/.ccr/README.md`) cannot re-terminate — the README's own unsupported-class list names exactly this ("certificate-pinned clients... If a tool still cannot work through the proxy, report it"). Confirmed it isn't a proxy-config gap: `CURL_CA_BUNDLE`/`SSL_CERT_FILE`/`REQUESTS_CA_BUNDLE` are all already correctly set to the proxy's CA bundle, and plain `curl`/OpenSSL reach Yahoo's endpoints fine (got a normal HTTP 429 rate-limit, not a TLS error). Tried a plain-`requests` fallback (bypassing `curl_cffi` entirely) directly against Yahoo's `quoteSummary` API: got HTTP 401 "Invalid Crumb" — Yahoo's own bot-detection now requires the cookie/crumb handshake that only the blocked `curl_cffi` TLS-impersonation path can complete, so this isn't fixable by routing around `curl_cffi`. Checked the Interactive Brokers MCP toolset for an alternative fundamentals source (income statement / balance sheet / cash flow / margins / ROIC): none exists — only price/options/themes/connections/account tools are exposed. Per CLAUDE.md Rule 0 ("never invent or estimate financial data — if a metric is missing, stop and ask") and this command's explicit unattended contingency, **the auto-commit for AAPL is skipped**: no Phase 01 gate, no score, no `sessions/` file, and no watchlist entry were created or committed for AAPL this run, since none of those criteria are obtainable from either approved data source in this environment. Flagged in GitHub issue for manual follow-up once a working fundamentals source is available (or the proxy/`curl_cffi` incompatibility is fixed) — `/new-position AAPL` should be re-run manually at that point; this is a genuine, identified gap, not a "no action" mention. |
